<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;text-align:center;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:23px;line-height:107%;">Questions &amp; Answers</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;text-align:center;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#00B050;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;text-align:center;'><strong><span style="font-size:21px;line-height:107%;color:#00B050;">Easy Questions</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;text-align:center;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#00B050;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 1:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name, last name, and gender of patients who&apos;s gender is &apos;M&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name, gender</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">gender= &apos;M&apos;;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 2:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name and last name of patients who does not have allergies. (null)</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies IS <span style="color:#0070C0;">NULL;</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 3:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name of patients that start with the letter &apos;C&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name <span style="color:#0070C0;">LIKE&nbsp;</span>&apos;C%&apos;;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">substring (first_name, 1, 1) = &apos;C&apos;;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 4:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name and last name of patients that weight within the range of 100 to 120 (inclusive)</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;patients&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">weight <span style="color:#0070C0;">BETWEEN&nbsp;</span>100 <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>120;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">weight &gt;= 100 <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>weight &lt;= 120;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 5:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Update the patients table for the allergies column. If the patient&apos;s allergies is null then replace it with &apos;NKA&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">UPDATE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SET&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies = &apos;NKA&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies <span style="color:#0070C0;">IS NULL</span>;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 6:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name and last name concatinated into one column to show their full name.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(first_name || &apos; &apos; || last_name) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>full_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">CONCAT&nbsp;</span>(first_name, &apos; &apos;, last_name) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>full_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 7:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name, last name, and the full province name of each patient.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Example: &apos;Ontario&apos; instead of &apos;ON&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients.first_name, patients.last_name, province_names.province_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_names</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients.province_id = province_names.province_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patient_id;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>


<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 8:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show how many patients have a birth_date with 2010 as the birth year.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT COUNT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(patient_id) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>total_patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">birth_date <span style="color:#0070C0;">LIKE&nbsp;</span>&apos;2010%&apos;;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">count(first_name) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>total_patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">city</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Write a query to find the first_name, last name and birth date of patients who have height more than 160 and weight more than 70.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Write a query to find list of patients first_name, last_name, and allergies from Hamilton where allergies are not null.</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 1:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show unique birth years from patients and order them by ascending.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT YEAR&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(birth_date) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>birth_year</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 2:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show unique first names from the patients table which only occurs once in the list.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">For example, if two or more people are named &apos;John&apos; in the first_name column then don&apos;t include their name in the output list. If only 1 person is named &apos;Leo&apos; then include them in the output.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">HAVING COUNT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(first_name) = 1;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;"><span style="text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</span></span></u></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY LENGTH&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(first_name), first_name <span style="color:#0070C0;">ASC</span>;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 6:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show the total amount of male patients and the total amount of female patients in the patients table.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Display the two results in the same row.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT SUM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(gender==&apos;M&apos;) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>male_count, <span style="color:#0070C0;">SUM&nbsp;</span>(gender==&apos;F&apos;) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>female_count</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; (<span style="color:#0070C0;">SELECT COUNT</span> (*) <span style="color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span>patients <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span>gender=&apos;M&apos;) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>male_count,&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; (<span style="color:#0070C0;">SELECT COUNT&nbsp;</span>(*) <span style="color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span>patients <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span>gender=&apos;F&apos;) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>female_count;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 7:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first and last name, allergies from patients which have allergies to either &apos;Penicillin&apos; or &apos;Morphine&apos;. Show results ordered ascending by allergies then by first_name then by last_name.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name, allergies</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies=&apos;Penicillin&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">OR&nbsp;</span>allergies = &apos;Morphine&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies, first_name, last_name <span style="color:#0070C0;">ASC</span>;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; allergies</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; allergies IN (&apos;Penicillin&apos;, &apos;Morphine&apos;)</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; allergies,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name, &nbsp; last_name, &nbsp;allergies</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHERE</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; allergies = &apos;Penicillin&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">OR&nbsp;</span>allergies = &apos;Morphine&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; allergies ASC,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name ASC,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name ASC;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 8:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show patient_id, diagnosis from admissions. Find patients admitted multiple times for the same diagnosis.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; patient_id,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; diagnosis</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">admissions</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">diagnosis, patient_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">HAVING COUNT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(diagnosis) &gt; 1;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;"><span style="text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</span></span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;"><span style="text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</span></span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 9:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show the city and the total number of patients in the city.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Order from most to least patients and then by city name ascending.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">city, <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(patient_id) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>num_patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">city&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY COUNT</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;(patient_id) <span style="color:#0070C0;">DESC</span>, city <span style="color:#0070C0;">ASC</span>;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 10:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first name, last name and role of every person that is either patient or doctor.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">The roles are either &quot;Patient&quot; or &quot;Doctor&quot;.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name, &apos;Patient&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>role <span style="color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span>patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">UNION ALL&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name, &apos;Doctor&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>role <span style="color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span>doctors;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 11:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show all allergies ordered by popularity. Remove NULL values from query.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; allergies,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(*)</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">allergies</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 12:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show all patient&apos;s first_name, last_name, and birth_date who were born in the 1970s decade. Sort the list starting from the earliest birth_date.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name,birth_date</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name, &nbsp; last_name, &nbsp;birth_date</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; birth_date &gt;= &apos;1970-01-01&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>birth_date &lt; &apos;1980-01-01&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">birth_date <span style="color:#0070C0;">ASC;</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 13:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">We want to display each patient&apos;s full name in a single column. Their last_name in all upper letters must appear first, then first_name in all lower case letters. Separate the last_name and first_name with a comma. Order the list by the first_name in decending order</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">EX: SMITH,jane</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT UPPER&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(last_name) ||&apos;,&apos;|| <span style="color:#0070C0;">LOWER&nbsp;</span>(first_name) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>new_name_format</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name <span style="color:#0070C0;">DESC</span>;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">CONCAT&nbsp;</span>(<span style="color:#0070C0;">UPPER&nbsp;</span>(last_name), &apos;,&apos;, <span style="color:#0070C0;">LOWER</span> (first_name)) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>new_name_format</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 14:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show the province_id(s), sum of height; where the total sum of its patient&apos;s height is greater than or equal to 7,000.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_id, <span style="color:#0070C0;">SUM&nbsp;</span>(height) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>sum_height</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">HAVING SUM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(height)&gt;=7000</span></p>
