<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>patient_id % 2 != 0</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; )</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">OR</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; (</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">LEN&nbsp;</span>(patient_id)=3</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; attending_doctor_id <span style="color:#0070C0;">LIKE&nbsp;</span>&apos;%2%&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; );</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 19:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show first_name, last_name, and total number of admissions attended for each doctor.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Every admission has been attended by a doctor.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">doctors.first_name, doctors.last_name, <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(admission_date)&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">doctors</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">admissions <span style="color:#0070C0;">ON&nbsp;</span>admissions.attending_doctor_id = doctors.doctor_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">attending_doctor_id;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;"><span style="text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</span></span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; last_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(*)</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; doctors p,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; admissions a</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">where</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; a.attending_doctor_id = p.doctor_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">p.doctor_id;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 20:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">For each doctor, display their id, full name, and the first and last admission date they attended.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; doctors.doctor_id,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; doctors.first_name||&apos; &apos;||doctors.last_name <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>full_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">MIN&nbsp;</span>(admissions.admission_date) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>first_admission_date,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">MAX&nbsp;</span>(admissions.admission_date) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>last_admission_date</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">doctors</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span>admissions on doctors.doctor_id = admissions.attending_doctor_id &nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">admissions.attending_doctor_id;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 21:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Display the total amount of patients for each province. Order by descending.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; province_names.province_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(patients.patient_id) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>patient_count</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_names</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span>patients <span style="color:#0070C0;">ON&nbsp;</span>patients.province_id = province_names.province_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients.province_id&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patient_count <span style="color:#0070C0;">DESC</span>;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 22:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">For every admission, display the patient&apos;s full name, their admission diagnosis, and their doctor&apos;s full name who diagnosed their problem.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; p.first_name || &apos; &apos; || p.last_name as patients_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; a.diagnosis,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; d.first_name||&apos; &apos;||d.last_name as doctor_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">admissions a</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients p <span style="color:#0070C0;">ON&nbsp;</span>p.patient_id &nbsp; = a.patient_id&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">doctors d <span style="color:#0070C0;">ON&nbsp;</span>d.doctor_id = a.attending_doctor_id;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 23:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Display the number of duplicate patients based on their first_name and last_name.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name, <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(*) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>num_of_duplicates</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">first_name, last_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">HAVING COUNT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(first_name and last_name) = 2;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 24:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Display patient&apos;s full name, height in the units feet rounded to 1 decimal,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">weight in the unit pounds rounded to 0 decimals, birth_date, gender non-abbreviated.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Convert CM to feet by dividing by 30.48.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Convert KG to pounds by multiplying by 2.205.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; first_name || &apos; &apos; || last_name <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>patient_name,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">ROUND&nbsp;</span>(height / 30.48, 1) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>&apos;height &quot;Feet&quot;&apos;,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">ROUND&nbsp;</span>(weight * 2.205, 0) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>&apos;weight &quot;Pound&quot;&apos;,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; birth_date,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">CASE</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHEN&nbsp;</span>gender = &apos;M&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN&nbsp;</span>&apos;MALE&apos;</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show all of the patients grouped into weight groups.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show the total amount of patients in each weight group.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Order the list by the weight group descending.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">For example, if they weight 100 to 109 they are placed in the 100 weight group, 110-119 = 110 weight group, etc.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">FLOOR&nbsp;</span>(weight/10)*10 <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>weight_group</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">TRUNCATE</span> (weight, -1) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>weight_group,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(*)</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Or,</span></u></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">COUNT&nbsp;</span>(patient_id),</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; weight - weight % 10 <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>weight_group</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ORDER BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">weight_group <span style="color:#0070C0;">DESC;</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 2:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show patient_id, weight, height, isObese from the patients table.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Display isObese as a boolean 0 or 1.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Obese is defined as weight(kg)/(height(m)2) &gt;= 30.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">weight is in units kg.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">height is in units cm.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; patient_id,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; weight,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; height,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">CASE</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHEN&nbsp;</span>(weight/power((height*.01),2))&gt;=30 <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN &nbsp;</span>1</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">ELSE&nbsp;</span>0</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">END AS&nbsp;</span>isObese</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; patient_id,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; weight,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; height,</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; weight / <span style="color:#0070C0;">POWER&nbsp;</span>(<span style="color:#0070C0;">CAST&nbsp;</span>(height <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>float) / 100, 2) &gt;= 30 <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>obese</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patients;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 3:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show patient_id, first_name, last_name, and attending doctor&apos;s specialty.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show only the patients who has a diagnosis as &apos;Epilepsy&apos; and the doctor&apos;s first name is &apos;Lisa&apos;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Check patients, admissions, and doctors tables for required information.</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">ELSE&nbsp;</span>&apos;No&apos;</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">SUM&nbsp;</span>(</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">CASE</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHEN&nbsp;</span>patient_id % 2 = 0 <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN&nbsp;</span>10</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;admissions <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHERE&nbsp;</span>patient_id % 2 = 1 <span style="color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span>has_insurance</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">UNION</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">ELSE COUNT&nbsp;</span>(has_insurance) * 50</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">END AS&nbsp;</span>cost_after_insurance</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">WHEN&nbsp;</span>patient_id % 2 = 0 <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN&nbsp;</span>&apos;Yes&apos;</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">has_insurance, <span style="color:#0070C0;">SUM&nbsp;</span>(admission_cost) <span style="color:#0070C0;">AS&nbsp;</span>admission_total</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">&nbsp; &nbsp;CASE WHEN&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">patient_id % 2 = 0 <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN&nbsp;</span>&apos;Yes&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">ELSE&nbsp;</span>&apos;No&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">END AS&nbsp;</span>has_insurance,</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp;<span style="color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span>admissions)</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 6:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show the provinces that has more patients identified as &apos;M&apos; than &apos;F&apos;. Must only show full province_name.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">pr.province_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_names pr</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">JOIN&nbsp;</span>patients pt <span style="color:#0070C0;">ON&nbsp;</span>pr.province_id = pt.province_id</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">GROUP BY&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">HAVING</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">SUM&nbsp;</span>(<span style="color:#0070C0;">CASE WHEN&nbsp;</span>gender = &apos;M&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN &nbsp;</span>1 <span style="color:#0070C0;">ELSE&nbsp;</span>0 <span style="color:#0070C0;">END</span>) &gt; <span style="color:#0070C0;">SUM&nbsp;</span>(<span style="color:#0070C0;">CASE WHEN&nbsp;</span>gender = &apos;F&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN&nbsp;</span>1 <span style="color:#0070C0;">ELSE&nbsp;</span>0 <span style="color:#0070C0;">END</span>);</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><u><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Or,</span></u></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">SELECT&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">province_name</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">FROM&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">(</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">SELECT</span></span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; province_name,</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND MONTH&nbsp;</span>(birth_date) <span style="color:#0070C0;">IN&nbsp;</span>(2, 5, 12)</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>weight <span style="color:#0070C0;">BETWEEN&nbsp;</span>60 <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>80</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">AND&nbsp;</span>city = &apos;Kingston&apos;;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Questions 8:&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Show the percent of patients that have &apos;M&apos; as their gender. Round the answer to the nearest hundredth number and in percent form.</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><strong><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">Solution:</span></strong></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">&nbsp; <span style="color:#0070C0;">CONCAT&nbsp;</span>(<span style="color:#0070C0;">ROUND&nbsp;</span>( &nbsp;(</span></p>

<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">WHEN&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;">gender = &apos;M&apos; <span style="color:#0070C0;">THEN&nbsp;</span>1&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-left:0in;line-height:107%;font-size:15px;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;'><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#0070C0;">ELSE&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size:19px;line-height:107%;color:#7030A0;">NULL&nbsp;</span></p>
